namespace = mbs_bastard

#Find secret bastard child
long_character_event  = {
	id = mbs_bastard.1
	desc = "EVTDESCmbs_bastard.1"
	picture = GFX_evt_child_play

	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 24
	only_men = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = { name = search_secretbastard value = on }
		is_lowborn = no
		is_theocracy = no
		NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
		NOT = {
			any_dynasty_member_even_if_dead  = {
				count = 2
				is_female = no
				is_alive = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = secret_bastard_come_forward
		}
		NOT = {
			character = 317
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = eunuch
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = homosexual
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {

		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			crownlaw_title = { has_law = first_night_1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			trait = celibate
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = secret_bastard_come_forward
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAmbs_bastard.1" #Yay!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2

			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				trait = honorable
			}
		}

		piety = -15
		hidden_tooltip = {
			spouse = {
				character_event = { id = 76101 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP308" } # The wife is angered
			}
		}
		location = {
			ROOT = {
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 0
							female = yes
							culture = ROOT
							religion = ROOT
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					50 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 0
							female = no
							culture = ROOT
							religion = ROOT
							historical = yes
						}
					}
				}
				new_character = {
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { is_female = no } }
						set_father = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { is_female = yes } }
						set_mother = ROOT
					}
					add_trait = bastard
					bastard_nickname_father_effect = yes
					dynasty = ROOT
					ROOT = {
						any_owned_bloodline = {
							PREVPREV = {
								add_to_bloodline = PREV
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { culture = high_valyrian }
						set_character_flag = high_valyrian
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { trait = clubfooted } }
						random = { chance = 15 add_trait = clubfooted }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { trait = harelip } }

					}

					random_list = {

	only_men = yes

			factor = 2

			factor = 1.3

			trait = gregarious

long_character_event  = {
	id = mbs_bastard.42
	desc = "EVTDESCmbs_bastard.42"
	picture = GFX_evt_council

	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 45
	only_men = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_game_rule = { name = search_secretbastard value = on }
		is_lowborn = no
		is_theocracy = no
		NOT_mythical_creature_trigger = yes
		NOT = {
			any_dynasty_member_even_if_dead  = {
				count = 2
				is_female = no
				is_alive = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_character_flag = secret_bastard_come_forward
		}
		NOT = {
			character = 317
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = eunuch
		}
		NOT = {
			trait = homosexual
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {

		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.3
			trait = gluttonous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			trait = gregarious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			crownlaw_title = { has_law = first_night_1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0

		}
	}

				character_event = { id = 76101 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP308" } # The wife is angered
			}
		}

				random_list = {
					50 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 25

							religion = ROOT
							historical = yes
						}
					}
					50 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 25
							female = no
							random_traits = yes
							culture = ROOT
							religion = ROOT
							historical = yes
						}
					}
				}
				new_character = {

						limit = { ROOT = { is_female = no } }
						set_father = ROOT
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { is_female = yes } }
						set_mother = ROOT

					add_trait = bastard

					dynasty = ROOT
